530.3(1): bstan pa 'di la lhag bsam can gyis phyar gru mnyam 'degs byas pa las byung ba 
530.4(1): yin/ kan su'u mi rigs dpe skrun khang gi dbu khrid 'brug rgyal mkhar dang gcod pa 
530.5(1): rnam gnyis nas thugs khur rgyab skyor tshad med gnang ba dang / lhag par du dus rab 
530.6(1): kyi gnyan 'phrang mang po'i nang tshe srog 'ben dang bsdos te srung skyong byas pa'i dpe cha 
530.7(1): g.yar ba'i dpe bdag rnam pa dang / de bzhin nga tsho'i bstan don gyi bya ba kun la 
530.8(1): mthun sbyor gnang ba ma tshad dpe tshogs 'di dpar skrun skabs su yang ma bskul dang 
530.9(1): blang gis zhal 'debs gnang mkhan bcas dngos shugs brgyud gsum nas rgyu tshegs 
530.10(1): thabs gsum gyis sdong grogs rogs ram gnang mkhan yongs la snying dbus nas
